     <div class="row">
      <section class="col-sm-12">
       <a id="main-content">
       </a>
       <div class="region region-content">
        <section class="block block-system clearfix" id="block-system-main">
         <div class="panel-display moscone-flipped clearfix ">
          <div class="moscone-container moscone-header clearfix panel-panel">
           <div class="moscone-container-inner moscone-header-inner panel-panel-inner">
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="moscone-flipped-container moscone-flipped-column-content clearfix">
           <div class="moscone-flipped-column-content-region moscone-flipped-content panel-panel">
            <div class="moscone-flipped-column-content-region-inner moscone-flipped-content-inner panel-panel-inner">
             <div class="panel-bootstrap-pane alert alert-default pane-panels-mini pane-home">
              <div class="alert-body">
               <div class="panel-display pond clearfix " id="mini-panel-home">
                <div class="pond-container pond-header clearfix panel-panel">
                 <div class="pond-container-inner pond-header-inner panel-panel-inner">
                  <div class="panel-bootstrap-pane jumbotron pane-block pane-block-20">
                   <div class="jumbotron-body">
                    <p>
                     Butterflies and Moths of North America (BAMONA) is an ambitious effort to collect, store, and share species information and occurrence data. You can participate by taking and submitting photographs of butterflies, moths, and caterpillars.
                    </p>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <div class="panel-separator">
                  </div>
                  <div class="panel-bootstrap-pane well pane-recent-sightings-1">
                   <div class="well-body">
                    <div id="leaflet-map-37286172" style="height: 360px">
                    </div>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="pond-container pond-column-content pond-column-content-row1 clearfix">
                 <div class="pond-column-content-region pond-column pond-column1 panel-panel">
                  <div class="pond-column-content-region-inner pond-column-inner pond-column1-inner panel-panel-inner">
                   <div class="panel-pane pane-custom pane-1">
                    <div class="pane-content">
                     <h2 align="center">
                      <span aria-hidden="true" class="glyphicon glyphicon-search">
                      </span>
                     </h2>
                     <p>
                      Explore the variety of moths and butterflies in North America. Browse
                      <a href="/checklists">
                       regional species checklists
                      </a>
                      and
                      <a href="/taxonomy">
                       taxonomy pages
                      </a>
                      or search the
                      <a href="/species_search">
                       species database
                      </a>
                      to find species profiles, distribution maps, and photographs.
                     </p>
                    </div>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="pond-column-content-region pond-column pond-column2 panel-panel">
                  <div class="pond-column-content-region-inner pond-column-inner pond-column2-inner panel-panel-inner">
                   <div class="panel-pane pane-custom pane-2">
                    <div class="pane-content">
                     <h2 align="center">
                      <span aria-hidden="true" class="glyphicon glyphicon-camera">
                      </span>
                     </h2>
                     <p>
                      <a href="/get-involved">
                       Get involved
                      </a>
                      in the project. Submit photographs of your sightings, or share your expertise and help us review and verify submissions.
                     </p>
                    </div>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="pond-column-content-region pond-column pond-column3 panel-panel">
                  <div class="pond-column-content-region-inner pond-column-inner pond-column3-inner panel-panel-inner">
                   <div class="panel-pane pane-custom pane-3">
                    <div class="pane-content">
                     <h2 align="center">
                      <span aria-hidden="true" class="glyphicon glyphicon-globe">
                      </span>
                     </h2>
                     <p>
                      Discover our maps and data. Find
                      <a href="/recent_sightings">
                       recently verified sightings
                      </a>
                      , or search and browse the
                      <a href="/explore-data">
                       sightings database
                      </a>
                      .
                     </p>
                    </div>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="pond-container pond-secondary-column-content pond-column-content-row2 clearfix">
                 <div class="pond-secondary-column-content-region pond-column pond-secondary-column1 panel-panel">
                  <div class="pond-secondary-column-content-region-inner pond-column-inner pond-secondary-column1-inner panel-panel-inner">
                   <div class="panel-pane pane-custom pane-4">
                    <div class="pane-content">
                     <h2 align="center">
                      <span aria-hidden="true" class="glyphicon glyphicon-info-sign">
                      </span>
                     </h2>
                     <p>
                      Learn more
                      <a href="about">
                       about this project
                      </a>
                      . We aim to fill the needs of scientists and nature observers by bringing verified occurrence and life history data into one location.
                     </p>
                    </div>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="pond-secondary-column-content-region pond-column pond-secondary-column2 panel-panel">
                  <div class="pond-secondary-column-content-region-inner pond-column-inner pond-secondary-column2-inner panel-panel-inner">
                   <div class="panel-pane pane-custom pane-5">
                    <div class="pane-content">
                     <h2 align="center">
                      <span aria-hidden="true" class="glyphicon glyphicon-question-sign">
                      </span>
                     </h2>
                     <p>
                      Get help
                      <a href="/identify">
                       identifying a butterfly, moth, or caterpillar
                      </a>
                      . It is a trade: you help us collect verifiable data, and we will try to identify the species.
                     </p>
                    </div>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
